msg:April Wu Village Baby Walk

Village activities are divided into four seasons (picking eggs, pig races, bonfire parties, etc.), indoor activities (hand-grinded soy milk, children's playhouses, swimming, etc.), and outdoor activities (tree climbing, happy cycling, Wu Village train, etc.). The details can be found on the "Wu Village Trip Assistant" applet.

There will be festival activities and decorations according to different festivals. I personally feel that there will be more activities during holidays and weekends when the occupancy rate is high, and the village will be more popular~

For the first time with a baby, I chose Daoshe Hotel for safety. Although it is outside the village, the shuttle bus shuttles frequently, and it is very convenient for children to like it. Next time I come, I may choose to try a more primitive village. We stayed on the weekend, the occupancy rate was high, the three meals were fresh, especially the vegetables and fruits were very fresh and delicious, the restaurant was very large, and it was unlikely that you could not find a seat when you arrived. The service staff in the hotel and the village were also very friendly to the children.

The children loved running back and forth between the houses and fields in the village. Even when they were not participating in any activities, they could still have fun by themselves, picking up leaves, listening to the chirping of insects, looking for snails after the rain... After all, the magic brought by nature will never let us down.

name:G‚Äçu‚Äçe‚Äçs‚Äçt‚Äç ‚ÄçU‚Äçs‚Äçe‚Äçr

posted:Posted February 24, 2024
msg:I chose this place for the last three days of the Spring Festival. There were many recommendations on Xiaohongshu, so that my little friends could experience the life in the village and the a**osphere of celebrating the New Year in a small town in the south of the Yangtze River~~~
In terms of transportation, navigate to the Wucun ticket office. It takes 1 hour and 45 minutes from Shanghai. The security guard at the entrance will ask where to go. Basically, the parking lot here can meet the parking needs of tourists. You can register at the door after getting off the car, and then enter the village to change attractions. We drove to the hotel, but actually walked 200 meters to the hotel, and then checked in as normal at the hotel front desk~~ Rooms were tight during the Spring Festival, and rooms were not available until almost 2 o'clock. From the check-in experience, the connection between the various links is relatively good, and parking is not directly accessible. The hotel has solved this problem well. The only discomfort is that it may be slightly inconvenient to carry luggage on rainy days. The road in the parking lot is a stone road and is not suitable for dragging suitcases~~~
The hotel rooms are relatively large and comfortable, and all have balconies. There are coffee tables and sofas on the balconies. The mineral water and minibars in the hotel are relatively complete, and the hardware conditions are very good~~~
In terms of sound insulation of the room, the sound insulation of the corridor is still relatively average. You can basically hear the sounds outside, and even the music played in the floor passage. It is recommended that the hotel turn down the volume in the afternoon. After all, it is a family hotel, and some children will I want to sleep; the sound insulation of the room is relatively good at night, and there is almost no sound from the next room, so the quality of sleep is not affected~~~
In terms of catering, the hotel itself only has a restaurant on the first floor. During the Spring Festival, it is a semi-self-service hot pot. Other catering is in Wucun, which requires a car. During the Spring Festival, it is basically a set meal. If you walk, you can walk there in about 10 minutes. There are several coffee bars. The quality is quite normal and the taste is good~~~ Or you can go to Wuzhen Xizha to eat, which is more convenient.
In terms of fun, the hotel itself has a swimming pool with a temperature of 30¬∞C. If you want to go from the guest room without leaving the hotel, you need to go around the second floor. There is also a book bar and table games;
There are many places for parents and children to visit in Wucun. There is a lawn, a small animal park, and children's play areas. The children's park is not big. This is the only area captured in the picture. There are also some entertainment equipment. There are many activities during the Spring Festival. , if you want to play at other times, look for the mini program on WeChat in advance~~
